Index Validation</strong>: Comprehensive validation system with intelligent suggestions</li>\n<li><strong>Model Context Protocol (MCP)</strong>: AI integration for automated market analysis with over 20 tools.</li>\n<li><strong>Endpoint-Level Caching</strong>: In-memory caching (10-minute TTL) for rapid responses to repeated queries.</li>\n<li><strong>HTTP Caching</strong>: All REST API responses include a <code>Cache-Control: public, max-age=30</code> header to reduce server load and improve client-side performance.</li>\n<li>Multiple data endpoints including:\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Price and Volume information</li>\n<li>Floorsheet Data</li>\n<li>Market Summary</li>\n<li>Live Market Data</li>\n<li>Top Gainers/Losers</li>\n<li>Company Details</li>\n<li>Sector-wise Information</li>\n<li>Index and Sub-indices</li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li><strong>Input Validation</strong>: All endpoints validate stock symbols and index names against actual NEPSE data</li>\n<li><strong>Containerized Deployment</strong>: Docker and Docker Compose support for easy deployment</li>\n<li><strong>Rate Limiting</strong>: Built-in protection against API abuse with configurable limits</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"><g-emoji class=\"g-emoji\" alias=\"warning\">⚠️</g-emoji> Important Legal &amp; dir=\"auto\">The project consists of three main components:</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>REST API Server</strong> (<code>server.py</code>)</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Built with FastAPI</li>\n<li>Provides HTTP endpoints for market data</li>\n<li>Runs on port 8000</li>\n<li>Supports CORS</li>\n<li>Uses uvicorn as the ASGI server</li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>WebSocket Server</strong> (<code>socketServer.py</code>)</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Provides real-time data streaming</li>\n<li>Supports bidirectional communication</li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>MCP Server</strong> (<code>mcp_server.py</code>) - <strong>NEW</strong></p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li>Model Context Protocol server for AI integration</li>\n<li>Provides structured access to all stock data endpoints</li>\n<li>Compatible with Claude Desktop and other MCP clients</li>\n<li>Enables AI models to query Nepal stock market data</li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Installation</h2><a id=\"user-content-installation\" id=\"user-content-websocket-server-usage\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: WebSocket Server Usage\" href=\"#websocket-server-usage\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">The WebSocket server provides a persistent, real-time connection for receiving NEPSE data. It's ideal for applications that need live updates without constant polling.</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>Connecting to the Server:</strong>\nConnect your WebSocket client to <code>ws://localhost:5555</code> (or <code>wss://nepseapiws.surajrimal.dev/</code> for the hosted version).</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>Communication Protocol:</strong>\nCommunication is done via JSON messages.</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Client Request</strong>: Send a JSON object with a <code>route</code> and optional <code>params</code>.</li>\n<li><strong>Server Response</strong>: The server will respond with the requested data or an error message in JSON format.</li>\n</ul>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>Example 1: Get Market Summary</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>Send this message to the server:</strong></p>\n<div class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\"><pre>{\n  <span class=\"pl-ent\">\"route\"</span>: <span class=\"pl-s\"><span class=\"pl-pds\">\"</span>Summary<span class=\"pl-pds\">\"</span></span>,\n  <span class=\"pl-ent\">\"params\"</span>: {}\n}</pre><div class=\"zeroclipboard-container\">\n    <clipboard-copy aria-label=\"Copy code to clipboard\" class=\"ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center\" data-copy-feedback=\"Copied!\" data-tooltip-direction=\"w\" value=\"{\n  &quot;route&quot;: &quot;Summary&quot;,\n  &quot;params&quot;: {}\n}\" tabindex=\"0\" role=\"button\">\n      <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" data-component=\"Octicon\" height=\"16\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" data-view-component=\"true\" class=\"octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon\">\n    <path d=\"M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z\"></path><path d=\"M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25
